   &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;A reconciliation of income taxes computed at&#13;the statutory rate is as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company applies Topic 718 &amp;#147;Share-Based&#13;Payments&amp;#148; (&amp;#147;Topic 718&amp;#148;) to share-based compensation, which requires the measurement of the cost of services received&#13;in exchange for an award of an equity instrument based on the grant-date fair value of the award. Compensation cost is recognized&#13;when the event occurs. The Black-Scholes option-pricing model is used to estimate the fair value of options granted.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company uses the asset and liability method&#13;of accounting for income taxes in accordance with ASC 740-10, &amp;#147;Accounting for Income Taxes.&amp;#148; Under this method, income&#13;tax expense is recognized for the amount of: (i) taxes payable or refundable for the current year; and, (ii) deferred tax consequences&#13;of temporary differences resulting from matters that have been recognized in an entity&amp;#146;s financial statements or tax returns.&#13;Deferred tax assets and liabilities are measured using enacted tax rates expected to apply to taxable income in the years in which&#13;those temporary differences are expected to be recovered or settled. The effect on deferred tax assets and liabilities of a change&#13;in tax rates is recognized in the results of operations in the period that includes the enactment date. A valuation allowance is&#13;provided to reduce the deferred tax assets reported if, based on the weight of available positive and negative evidence, it is&#13;more likely than not that some portion or all of the deferred tax assets will not be realized.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Long-lived assets such as property and equipment&#13;are stated at their fair value acquisition cost and reviewed for impairment whenever facts and circumstances indicate that the&#13;carrying value may not be recoverable. Amortization of long-lived assets are calculated by the straight line method over their&#13;estimated useful lives. When required impairment losses on assets to be held and used are recognized based on the fair value of&#13;the asset. The fair value is determined based on estimates of future cash flows, market value of similar assets, if available,&#13;or independent appraisals, if required. If the carrying amount of the long-lived asset is not recoverable from its undiscounted&#13;cash flows, an impairment loss is recognized for the difference between the carrying amount and fair value of the asset. When fair&#13;values are not available, the Company estimates fair value using the expected future cash flows discounted at a rate commensurate&#13;with the risk associated with the recovery of the assets.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Depreciation is computed for financial statement&#13;purposes on a straight-line basis over estimated useful lives of the related assets. The estimated useful lives of depreciable&#13;assets are:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=width: 100%; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal&gt;&#13;&lt;tr&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 75%&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; width: 5%; font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=width: 20%; font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; text-align: center&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Estimated&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=border-bottom-style: solid; border-bottom-width: 1pt; font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; text-align: center&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Useful Lives&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=background-color: #CCEEFF&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: top; font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Equipment&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; text-align: center&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;5-10 years&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;For federal income tax purposes, depreciation&#13;is computed under the modified accelerated cost recovery system. For financial statements purposes, depreciation is computed under&#13;the straight-line method.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company's financial instruments consist&#13;primarily of cash, prepaid expense, deferred financing cost, accounts payable and accrued liabilities, accrued expenses, convertible&#13;notes and Note payable. The carrying amounts of such financial instruments approximate their respective estimated fair value due&#13;to the short-term maturities and approximate market interest rates of these instruments.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The Company adopted ASC Topic 820, Fair Value&#13;Measurements (&amp;#34;ASC Topic 820&amp;#34;), which defines fair value, establishes a framework for measuring fair value, and expands&#13;disclosures about fair value measurements. The standard provides a consistent definition of fair value which focuses on an exit&#13;price that would be received upon sale of an asset or paid to transfer a liability in an orderly transaction between market participants&#13;at the measurement date. The standard also prioritizes, within the measurement of fair value, the use of market-based information&#13;over entity specific information and establishes a three-level hierarchy for fair value measurements based on the nature of inputs&#13;used in the valuation of an asset or liability as of the measurement date.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The three-level hierarchy for fair value measurements&#13;is defined as follows:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Level 1 &amp;#150; inputs to the valuation methodology&#13;are quoted prices (unadjusted) for identical assets or liabilities in active markets; liabilities in active markets;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Level 2 &amp;#150; inputs to the valuation methodology&#13;include quoted prices for similar assets and liabilities in active markets, and inputs that are observable for the asset or liability&#13;other than quoted prices, either directly or indirectly, including inputs in markets that are not considered to be active; or directly&#13;or indirectly including inputs in markets that are not considered to be active;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;Level 3 &amp;#150; inputs to the valuation methodology&#13;are unobservable and significant to the fair value measurement&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;The following table summarizes fair value measurements&#13;by level at May 31, 2016, and 2015, measured at fair value on a recurring basis:&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; width: 100%; font-size-adjust: none; font-stretch: normal&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=vertical-align: bottom&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;May 31, 2016&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td colspan=2 id=hdcell style=border-bottom: black 1pt solid; text-align: center&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Level 1&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td colspan=2 style=border-bottom: black 1pt solid; text-align: center&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Level 2&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td colspan=2 style=border-bottom: black 1pt solid; text-align: center&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Level 3&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td colspan=2 style=border-bottom: black 1pt solid; text-align: center&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Total&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: top; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;&lt;b&gt;Liabilities&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td colspan=2 id=ffcell style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: right&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td colspan=2 style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: right&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td colspan=2 style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: right&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td colspan=2 style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: right&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr style=background-color: #CCEEFF&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: top; width: 389px; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Derivative liabilities&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;-&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;-&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;2,039,179&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: right&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;2,039,179&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; text-align: justify&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;tr&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;&lt;/tr&gt;&#13;&lt;/table&gt;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;table cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0 style=font: 12pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In November 2015, the FASB issued (ASU) 2015-17,&#13;&amp;#147;Balance Sheet Classification of Deferred Taxes.&amp;#148; Currently deferred taxes for each tax jurisdiction are presented&#13;as a net current asset or liability and net noncurrent asset or liability on the balance sheet. To simplify the presentation, the&#13;new guidance requires that deferred tax liabilities and assets for all jurisdictions along with any related valuation allowances&#13;be classified as noncurrent in a classified statement of financial position. This guidance is effective for interim and annual&#13;reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2016, and early adoption is permitted. The Company has adopted this guidance in&#13;the fourth quarter of the year ended December 31, 2015 on a retrospective basis. The adoption of this guidance did not have a material&#13;impact on the Company&amp;#146;s financial position, results of operations or cash flows, and did not have any effect on prior periods&#13;due to the full valuation allowance against the Company&amp;#146;s net deferred tax assets.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;i&gt;Recent Accounting Pronouncements Issued&#13;But Not Adopted as of May 31, 2016&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In March 2016, the FASB issued ASU 2016-09,&#13;&amp;#147;Compensation - Stock Compensation (Topic 718): Improvements to Employee Share-Based Payment Accounting&amp;#148;. The amendments&#13;are effective for public companies for annual periods beginning after December 15, 2016, and interim periods within those annual&#13;periods. Several aspects of the accounting for share-based payment award transactions are simplified, including: (a) income tax&#13;consequences; (b) classification of awards as either equity or liabilities; and (c) classification on the statement of cash flows.&#13;The Company is currently in the process of evaluating the impact of the adoption on its financial statements.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In February 2016, the FASB issued ASU No. 2016-02,&#13;&amp;#147;Leases (Topic 842)&amp;#148; (&amp;#147;ASU 2016-02&amp;#148;). ASU 2016-02 requires an entity to recognize assets and liabilities&#13;arising from a lease for both financing and operating leases. The ASU will also require new qualitative and quantitative disclosures&#13;to help investors and other financial statement users better understand the amount, timing, and uncertainty of cash flows arising&#13;from leases. ASU 2016-02 is effective for fiscal years beginning after December 15, 2018, with early adoption permitted. The Company&#13;is currently evaluating the impact of adopting this guidance.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In January 2016, the FASB issued ASU 2016-01,&#13;which amends the guidance in U.S. GAAP on the classification and measurement of financial instruments. Changes to the current guidance&#13;primarily affect the accounting for equity investments, financial liabilities under the fair value option, and the presentation&#13;and disclosure requirements for financial instruments. In addition, the ASU clarifies guidance related to the valuation allowance&#13;assessment when recognizing deferred tax assets resulting from unrealized losses on available-for-sale debt securities. The new&#13;standard is effective for fiscal years and interim periods beginning after December 15, 2017, and upon adoption, an entity should&#13;apply the amendments by means of a cumulative-effect adjustment to the balance sheet at the beginning of the first reporting period&#13;in which the guidance is effective. Early adoption is not permitted except for the provision to record fair value changes for financial&#13;liabilities under the fair value option resulting from instrument-specific credit risk in other comprehensive income. The Company&#13;is currently evaluating the impact of adopting this guidance.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In September 2015, the FASB issued ASU 2015-16,&#13;&amp;#147;Simplifying the Accounting for Measurement &amp;#150;Period Adjustments.&amp;#148; Changes to the accounting for measurement-period&#13;adjustments relate to business combinations. Currently, an acquiring entity is required to retrospectively adjust the balance sheet&#13;amounts of the acquiree recognized at the acquisition date with a corresponding adjustment to goodwill as a result of changes made&#13;to the balance sheet amounts of the acquiree. The measurement period is the period after the acquisition date during which the&#13;acquirer may adjust the balance sheet amounts recognized for a business combination (generally up to one year from the date of&#13;acquisition). The changes eliminate the requirement to make such retrospective adjustments, and, instead require the acquiring&#13;entity to record these adjustments in the reporting period they are determined. The new standard is effective for both public and&#13;private companies for periods beginning after December 15, 2015. The Company is currently evaluating the impact of adopting this&#13;guidance.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In August 2015, the FASB issued ASU No. 2015-14,&#13;Revenue From Contracts With Customers (Topic 606).&amp;#34; The amendments in this ASU defer the effective date of ASU 2014-09. Public&#13;business entities should apply the guidance in ASU 2014-09 to annual reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2017, including&#13;interim reporting periods within that reporting period. Earlier application is permitted only as of annual reporting periods beginning&#13;after December 15, 2016, including interim reporting periods within that reporting period. We are still evaluating the effect of&#13;the adoption of ASU 2014-09.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In April 2015, the FASB issued ASU 2015-05,&#13;&amp;#34;Intangibles - Goodwill and Other - Internal-Use Software (Subtopic 350-40): Customer's Accounting for Fees Paid in a Cloud&#13;Computing Arrangement,&amp;#34; which provides guidance about whether a cloud computing arrangement includes a software license. If&#13;a cloud computing arrangement includes a software license, the customer should account for the software license element of the&#13;arrangement consistent with the acquisition of other software licenses. If a cloud computing arrangement does not include a software&#13;license, the customer should account for the arrangement as a service contract. This ASU is effective for annual periods, including&#13;interim periods within those annual periods, beginning after December 15, 2015, and early adoption is permitted. The Company is&#13;currently evaluating the impact of adopting this guidance.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify&gt;In April 2015, the FASB issued guidance related&#13;to a customer&amp;#146;s accounting for fees paid in a cloud computing arrangement. This standard provides guidance to customers about&#13;whether a cloud computing arrangement includes a software license. If a cloud computing arrangement includes a software license,&#13;then the customer should account for the software license element of the arrangement consistent with the acquisition of other software&#13;licenses. If a cloud computing arrangement does not include a software license, the customer should account for the arrangement&#13;as a service contract. This guidance is effective for interim and annual reporting periods beginning after December 15, 2015, and&#13;early adoption is permitted. The Company will adopt this guidance on January 1, 2016. The adoption of this guidance is not expected&#13;to have a material impact on its financial position, results of operations or cash flows.&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
 Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; text-indent: 0.5in&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/p&gt;&#13;&#13;&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times
&lt;p style=font: 10pt Times New Roman
 Times

 Times

 Times
 Serif; text-align: justify&gt;&lt;font style=font-size: 10pt&gt;Equipment&lt;/font&gt;&lt;/td&gt;&#13;    &lt;td style=vertical-align: bottom; font: 12pt Times New Roman

var Show = {};
Show.LastAR = null
Show.hideAR = function(){
	Show.LastAR.style.display = 'none';
};
Show.showAR = function ( link
 id
 win ){
	if( Show.LastAR ){
		Show.hideAR();
	}
	var ref = link;
	do {
		ref = ref.nextSibling;
	} while (ref && ref.nodeName != 'TABLE');
	if (!ref || ref.nodeName != 'TABLE') {
		var tmp = win ?
			win.document.getElementById(id) :
			document.getElementById(id);
		if( tmp ){
			ref = tmp.cloneNode(true);
			ref.id = '';
			link.parentNode.appendChild(ref);
		}
	}
	if( ref ){
		ref.style.display = 'block';
		Show.LastAR = ref;
	}
};
Show.toggleNext = function( link ){
	var ref = link;
	do{
		ref = ref.nextSibling;
	}while( ref.nodeName != 'DIV' );
	if( ref.style &&
		ref.style.display &&
		ref.style.display == 'none' ){
		ref.style.display = 'block';
		if( link.textContent ){
			link.textContent = link.textContent.replace( '+'
 '-' );
		}else{
			link.innerText = link.innerText.replace( '+'
 '-' );
		}
	}else{
		ref.style.display = 'none';
		if( link.textContent ){
			link.textContent = link.textContent.replace( '-'
 '+' );
		}else{
			link.innerText = link.innerText.replace( '-'
 '+' );
		}
	}
};
